<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагрузить.html>нагрузи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nagruzítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагружать.html>нагружа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nagružátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагрузить.html>нагрузи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to load <i>(with)</i>, to lade <i>(with)</i>, to freight <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to load <i>(with)</i>, to saddle <i>(with)</i>, to lumber <i>(with)</i></li></ol>

***нагрузка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нагрузка.html>нагру́зка</a> (4485)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагрузить.html>нагрузи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nagruzítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагрузка.html>нагру́зка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nagrúzka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагрузка.html>нагру́зки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагрузка.html>нагру́зки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагрузка.html>нагру́зок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>loading</li>
<li>load, workload
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преподавательский.html>преподава́тельская</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нагрузка.html>нагру́зка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prepodavátelʹskaja <b>nagrúzka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">teaching <b>load</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неполный.html>непо́лная</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагрузка.html>нагру́зка</a></strong></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nepólnaja nagrúzka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">part-time</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">incomplete <b>load</b></span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering<span class="ib-comma">,</span> medicine<span class="ib-comma">,</span> electrical engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> load
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полезный.html>поле́зная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нагрузка.html>нагру́зка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">poléznaja <b>nagrúzka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">pay<b>load</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нагрузка.html>нагру́зка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rabóčaja <b>nagrúzka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">working <b>load</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нагрузка.html>нагру́зка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ось.html>ось</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nagrúzka</b> na osʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">axle <b>load</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нагрузка.html>нагру́зка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:линия.html>ли́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:связь.html>свя́зи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nagrúzka</b> línii svjázi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">traffic <b>load</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смысловой.html>смыслова́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нагрузка.html>нагру́зка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">smyslovája <b>nagrúzka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">meaning; message</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">semantic <b>load</b></span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>condition, stipulation <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">especially to purchase something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нагрянуть.html>нагря́нуть</a> (11484)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грянуть.html>гря́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grjánutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагрянуть.html>нагря́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nagrjánutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come unexpectedly (out of the blue)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нагрянуть.html>нагря́нули</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>го́сти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nagrjánuli</b> gósti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">guests arrived unexpectedly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break out, <i>(cold)</i> to strike</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грянуть.html>гря́нуть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">grjánutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грядущий.html>гряду́щий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">grjadúščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***над.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> (137)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nad</span>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental case</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>above, over</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Before words beginning with certain awkward consonant clusters such as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мн-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mn-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вс-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vs-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сн-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sn-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the variant form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nado</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used.
</p>

***надавить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надавить.html>надави́ть</a> (12951)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">davítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надавить.html>надави́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadavítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нада́вливать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to press, to push
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надавить.html>надави́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кнопка.html>кно́пку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadavítʹ</b> na knópku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to push/press the button</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to exert pressure <i>(on)</i>, to pressurize <i>(into)</i>, to pressure <i>(into)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">надвига́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadvigátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надвинуться.html>надви́нуться</a> (15616)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надвинуть.html>надви́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadvínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надвинуться.html>надви́нуться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadvínutʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надвигаться.html>надвига́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to approach, to draw near, to impend, to be imminent</li>
<li>to come <i>(over)</i>, to move <i>(onto)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надвинуть.html>надви́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadvínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">approach</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приблизиться.html>прибли́зиться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">priblízitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подступить.html>подступи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podstupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">come over</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подступить.html>подступи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podstupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***надвое.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надвое.html>на́двое</a> (14906)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>дво́е</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvóje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надвое.html>на́двое</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nádvoje</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>in two, in half, into two parts
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>дорога</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разделиться.html>раздели́лась</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:надвое.html>на́двое</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">doroga razdelílasʹ <b>nádvoje</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the road forked</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ambiguously, with a double meaning
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабушка.html>ба́бушка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надвое.html>на́двое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bábuška nádvoje skazála</i> ― <span class="e-translation">we'll see what we'll see; you never can tell</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надгробный.html>надгро́бный</a> (24327)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">над-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nad-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроб.html>гроб</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grob</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надгробный.html>надгро́бный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadgróbnyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>located on or over a grave</li>
<li>located or made on a gravestone
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надгробный.html>надгро́бная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:надпись.html>на́дпись</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadgróbnaja</b> nádpisʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>gravestone</b> inscription</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>funerary <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">speech, weeping, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надевать.html>надева́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<tbody><tr>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жда</a> (718)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жда</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadežda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nadeďa</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">надёжа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadjóža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жда</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadéžda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hope, expectation, prospect
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тщетный.html>тще́тные</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жды</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tščétnyje <b>nadéždy</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">vain <b>hopes</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***надел.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надел.html>наде́л</a> (2761)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надел.html>наде́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadél</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надел.html>наде́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надел.html>наде́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надел.html>наде́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(<i>historical</i>) Allotment land, which was the designation for pieces of land granted to peasants by their former landlords and the state with the reforms of the 1860s. The allotment lands had minimum and maximum sizes and were usually collectively owned.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надел.html>наде́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadél</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">masculine singular past indicative perfective of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надеть.html>наде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наделённый.html>наделённый</a> (7829)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наделённый.html>наделённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadeljónnyj</span>)

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наделить.html>надели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***наделать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наделать.html>наде́лать</a> (7239)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">délatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наделать.html>наде́лать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadélatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наде́лывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(certain quantity)</i> to make, to churn out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give, to cause
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наделать.html>наде́лать</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:хлопоты.html>хлопо́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadélatʹ</b> komú-libo xlopót</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give smb (a lot of) trouble</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наделать.html>наде́лать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ошибка.html>оши́бок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadélatʹ</b> ošíbok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a lot of mistakes/blunders</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наделать.html>наде́лать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глупость.html>глу́постей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadélatʹ</b> glúpostej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to commit follies</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наделать.html>наде́лать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:беда.html>беды</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadélatʹ</b> bedy/del</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a lot of trouble</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наделать.html>наде́лал</a></b>!; <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наделать.html>наде́лали</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">što ty <b>nadélal</b>!; što vy <b>nadélali</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what have you done!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наделать.html>наде́лать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шум.html>шу́ма</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:произвести.html>произвести́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сенсация.html>сенса́цию</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadélatʹ</b> mnógo šúma (proizvestí sensáciju)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cause a sensation/stir</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***наделить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наделить.html>надели́ть</a> (7829)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делить.html>дели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">delítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наделить.html>надели́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadelítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наделять.html>наделя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to allot, to give, to provide
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наделить.html>надели́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:подарок.html>пода́рками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadelítʹ</b> podárkami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dispense gifts</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наделить.html>надели́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>вла́стью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadelítʹ</b> vlástʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to confer powers; vest rights</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наделить.html>надели́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:полномочие.html>полномо́чиями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadelítʹ</b> polnomóčijami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to authorize; delegate authority</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to endow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наделённый.html>наделена́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:красота.html>красото́й</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>умо́м</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oná nadelená i krasotój, i umóm</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">she is endowed with both beauty and brains</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:природа.html>приро́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:щедро.html>ще́дро</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наделить.html>надели́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">priróda ščédro <b>nadelíla</b> jevó</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">nature has not spared her gifts to him</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***наделять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наделять.html>наделя́ть</a> (24987)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наделить.html>надели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наделять.html>наделя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadeljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наделить.html>надели́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to allot, to give, to provide
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наделять.html>наделя́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:подарок.html>пода́рками</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadeljátʹ</b> podárkami</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to dispense gifts</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наделять.html>наделя́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>вла́стью</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadeljátʹ</b> vlástʹju</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to confer powers; vest rights</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наделять.html>наделя́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:полномочие.html>полномо́чиями</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadeljátʹ</b> polnomóčijami</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to authorize; delegate authority</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to endow</li></ol>
